\doxysection{HTTP Modules}
\hypertarget{group__http}{}\label{group__http}\index{HTTP Modules@{HTTP Modules}}


Complete HTTP/1.\+1 and HTTP/2 protocol implementation with client and server support.

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Complete HTTP/1.\+1 and HTTP/2 protocol implementation with client and server support. 

The HTTP group provides comprehensive HTTP protocol support including parsing, serialization, client/server implementations, and advanced features. Key components include\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Socket\+HTTP (core)\+: HTTP types, headers, URI parsing, status codes
\item Socket\+HTTP1 (http1)\+: HTTP/1.\+1 parsing and serialization
\item Socket\+HTTP2 (http2)\+: HTTP/2 protocol implementation
\item \doxylink{structSocketHTTPClient}{Socket\+HTTPClient} (client)\+: High-\/level HTTP client with pooling
\item \doxylink{structSocketHTTPServer}{Socket\+HTTPServer} (server)\+: HTTP server implementation
\item Socket\+HPACK (hpack)\+: HTTP/2 header compression
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
foundation for base infrastructure. 

core\+\_\+io for socket primitives. 

security for TLS integration. 

\doxylink{group__http_gaba14ae9994f5645e5aa8488f905aad54}{Socket\+HTTPClient\+\_\+T} for HTTP client usage. 

\doxylink{group__http_gad59859e8ae07bfb95f5807590dd034f4}{Socket\+HTTPServer\+\_\+T} for HTTP server implementation. 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

Creates a thread-\/local copy of the exception with reason from socket\+\_\+error\+\_\+buf. Thread-\/safe\+: prevents race conditions when multiple threads raise same exception type.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{http2\_flow\_available\_send()}{http2\_flow\_available\_send()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t http2\+\_\+flow\+\_\+available\+\_\+send (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{group__http_ga71710b60048bb252c74115f947f14e6a}{Socket\+HTTP2\+\_\+\+Conn\+\_\+T}}}]{conn,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{group__http_gaae451408b4b91d69d78281b872773000}{Socket\+HTTP2\+\_\+\+Stream\+\_\+T}}}]{stream }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Thread-\/safe\+: Yes -\/ read-\/only. 

http2\+\_\+flow\+\_\+available\+\_\+send -\/ Get available send window @conn\+: Connection (const) @stream\+: Stream (may be NULL for connection-\/only, const)

Returns\+: Minimum of connection and stream windows, clamped to \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}=0 

Validates stream belongs to conn if provided. \Hypertarget{group__http_gae2f0b8ff528dfcd4951ea76392f84f9c}\label{group__http_gae2f0b8ff528dfcd4951ea76392f84f9c} 
\index{HTTP Modules@{HTTP Modules}!httpclient\_auth\_bearer\_header@{httpclient\_auth\_bearer\_header}}
\index{httpclient\_auth\_bearer\_header@{httpclient\_auth\_bearer\_header}!HTTP Modules@{HTTP Modules}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{httpclient\_auth\_bearer\_header()}{httpclient\_auth\_bearer\_header()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int httpclient\+\_\+auth\+\_\+bearer\+\_\+header (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{token,  }\item[{char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{output,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{output\+\_\+size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Thread-\/safe\+: Yes. 

httpclient\+\_\+auth\+\_\+bearer\+\_\+header -\/ Generate Bearer token Authorization header @token\+: Bearer token string @output\+: Output buffer for "{}\+Bearer $<$token$>$"{} @output\+\_\+size\+: Size of output buffer

Returns\+: 0 on success, -\/1 if buffer too small 

Format per RFC 6750\+: Authorization\+: Bearer $<$token$>$ Token is copied as-\/is, no validation or encoding. Token length limited by output\+\_\+size -\/ 7. \Hypertarget{group__http_ga945f44e73f0a313402745875d9102d1f}\label{group__http_ga945f44e73f0a313402745875d9102d1f}

Parse data incrementally. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em parser} & Parser instance \\
\hline
{\em data} & Input data buffer \\
\hline
{\em len} & Data length \\
\hline
{\em consumed} & Output -\/ bytes consumed from input \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
HTTP1\+\_\+\+OK when headers complete, HTTP1\+\_\+\+INCOMPLETE if need more, or error code @threadsafe No
\end{DoxyReturn}
Feed data to the parser incrementally. Can be called multiple times with partial data. Parsing stops at message boundary\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item After headers for HEAD responses, 1xx, 204, 304
\item After body for other responses
\item After headers for requests (body read separately) 
\end{DoxyItemize}\Hypertarget{group__http_gae0a96206e67a279005be9686d159faf3}\label{group__http_gae0a96206e67a279005be9686d159faf3}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SocketHTTP\_date\_parse()}{SocketHTTP\_date\_parse()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int Socket\+HTTP\+\_\+date\+\_\+parse (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{date\+\_\+str,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{len,  }\item[{time\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{time\+\_\+out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Parse HTTP-\/date. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em date\+\_\+str} & Date string in any valid HTTP-\/date format \\
\hline
{\em len} & Length of string (0 for strlen) \\
\hline
{\em time\+\_\+out} & Output time\+\_\+t (UTC) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, -\/1 on error @threadsafe Yes
\end{DoxyReturn}
Accepts three formats per RFC 9110\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item IMF-\/fixdate\+: Sun, 06 Nov 1994 08\+:49\+:37 GMT (preferred)
\item RFC 850\+: Sunday, 06-\/Nov-\/94 08\+:49\+:37 GMT (obsolete)
\item ANSI C\+: Sun Nov 6 08\+:49\+:37 1994 (obsolete) 
\end{DoxyItemize}\Hypertarget{group__http_ga9cd7416c4d2d906c57303c814cfffa05}\label{group__http_ga9cd7416c4d2d906c57303c814cfffa05}

Per RFC 9110, header names are tokens (tchar characters only). \Hypertarget{group__http_gafcd22b68210c4a6e922bbb88f34caacd}\label{group__http_gafcd22b68210c4a6e922bbb88f34caacd} 
\index{HTTP Modules@{HTTP Modules}!SocketHTTP\_header\_value\_valid@{SocketHTTP\_header\_value\_valid}}
\index{SocketHTTP\_header\_value\_valid@{SocketHTTP\_header\_value\_valid}!HTTP Modules@{HTTP Modules}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SocketHTTP\_header\_value\_valid()}{SocketHTTP\_header\_value\_valid()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int Socket\+HTTP\+\_\+header\+\_\+value\+\_\+valid (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{value,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{len }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Validate header value. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em value} & Header value \\
\hline
{\em len} & Value length \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if valid (no NUL/\+CR/\+LF), 0 otherwise @threadsafe Yes
\end{DoxyReturn}
SECURITY\+: Rejects NUL, CR, and LF characters to prevent HTTP header injection attacks (CWE-\/113). Per RFC 9110 Section 5.\+5, obs-\/fold (CRLF followed by SP/\+HTAB) is deprecated and should not be generated.

This stricter validation prevents\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item CRLF injection for header manipulation
\item Response splitting attacks
\item Cache poisoning via injected headers
\item Session hijacking via injected Set-\/\+Cookie 
\end{DoxyItemize}\Hypertarget{group__http_ga564aa2d79c404e093b07c56e7d7910eb}\label{group__http_ga564aa2d79c404e093b07c56e7d7910eb}

\index{HTTP Modules@{HTTP Modules}!SocketHTTPClient\_error\_is\_retryable@{SocketHTTPClient\_error\_is\_retryable}}
\index{SocketHTTPClient\_error\_is\_retryable@{SocketHTTPClient\_error\_is\_retryable}!HTTP Modules@{HTTP Modules}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SocketHTTPClient\_error\_is\_retryable()}{SocketHTTPClient\_error\_is\_retryable()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int Socket\+HTTPClient\+\_\+error\+\_\+is\+\_\+retryable (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{SocketHTTPClient_8h_a6b0f544308db17e698b4c05ac3358b75}{Socket\+HTTPClient\+\_\+\+Error}}}]{error }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Check if error code is retryable. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em error} & Error code from async operation\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if error is typically retryable, 0 if fatal @threadsafe Yes (pure function)
\end{DoxyReturn}
Use this to decide whether to retry a failed request\+:

Example\+: Socket\+HTTPClient\+\_\+\+Error err = Socket\+HTTPClient\+\_\+\+Request\+\_\+error(req); if (Socket\+HTTPClient\+\_\+error\+\_\+is\+\_\+retryable(err)) // Schedule retry with exponential backoff else // Log error and give up

Retryable errors\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item DNS failures (server may recover)
\item Connection failures (server may restart)
\item Timeouts (network may clear) 
\end{DoxyItemize}\Hypertarget{group__http_ga859120de13b0764564f3c1ce111b3379}\label{group__http_ga859120de13b0764564f3c1ce111b3379}

Begin graceful shutdown. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em server} & Server instance @timeout\+\_\+ms Maximum time to wait for requests to complete (-\/1 = infinite)\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Begins draining the server\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Stops accepting new connections
\item Existing connections continue processing
\item After timeout, force-\/closes remaining connections
\end{DoxyItemize}

\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int Socket\+HTTPServer\+\_\+\+Request\+\_\+begin\+\_\+stream (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__http_ga071a3760545fbd5fca4c2df224af0fad}{Socket\+HTTPServer\+\_\+\+Request\+\_\+T}}}]{req }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Begin streaming response. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em req} & Request context\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Begins a chunked transfer-\/encoding response. After calling\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Response headers are sent with Transfer-\/\+Encoding\+: chunked
\item Use send\+\_\+chunk() to send body data
\item Use end\+\_\+stream() to complete the response
\item Do NOT call body\+\_\+data(), body\+\_\+string(), or finish()
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, -\/1 on error @threadsafe No 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Enable streaming body callback. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em req} & Request context \\
\hline
{\em callback} & Callback invoked for each body chunk @userdata User data passed to callback\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Enables streaming mode for receiving request body. When enabled\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Body chunks are delivered via callback as they arrive
\item Body is NOT buffered in memory
\item \doxylink{group__http_ga7e95ae3464cb9cf8c0d0b172db13456e}{Socket\+HTTPServer\+\_\+\+Request\+\_\+body()} returns NULL
\end{DoxyItemize}

Call this before calling finish() to receive body data. @threadsafe No \Hypertarget{group__http_ga26d33e6cf21f83cbd542b1d5a41e7bca}\label{group__http_ga26d33e6cf21f83cbd542b1d5a41e7bca}

Set rate limiter for endpoint. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline

\hline
{\em limiter} & Rate limiter instance\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Socket\+HPACK\+\_\+\+Error -\/ General HPACK operation failure. 

Raised when\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Invalid header block encoding
\item Huffman decoding error
\item Integer overflow
\item Size limits exceeded
\item HPACK bomb detected

Use for general errors in HTTP core utilities. Specific errors should use module exceptions like Socket\+HTTP1\+\_\+\+Parse\+Error for parsers. \Hypertarget{group__http_ga83bda6e77bc5fb165e4e7fead483094b}\label{group__http_ga83bda6e77bc5fb165e4e7fead483094b} 
\index{HTTP Modules@{HTTP Modules}!SocketHTTPClient\_ConnectFailed@{SocketHTTPClient\_ConnectFailed}}
\index{SocketHTTPClient\_ConnectFailed@{SocketHTTPClient\_ConnectFailed}!HTTP Modules@{HTTP Modules}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SocketHTTPClient\_ConnectFailed}{SocketHTTPClient\_ConnectFailed}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily const Except\+\_\+T Socket\+HTTPClient\+\_\+\+Connect\+Failed\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



TCP connection failure. 

Category\+: NETWORK Retryable\+: YES -\/ Server may restart, network may recover

Raised when TCP connect() fails. Common causes\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item ECONNREFUSED\+: Server not listening (may start later)
\item ENETUNREACH\+: Network route unavailable (may recover)
\item EHOSTUNREACH\+: Host unreachable (may become reachable) 
\end{DoxyItemize}\Hypertarget{group__http_ga50039c8c595271d7d51b28ed5a4e7196}\label{group__http_ga50039c8c595271d7d51b28ed5a4e7196}

\index{SocketHTTPClient\_DNSFailed@{SocketHTTPClient\_DNSFailed}!HTTP Modules@{HTTP Modules}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SocketHTTPClient\_DNSFailed}{SocketHTTPClient\_DNSFailed}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily const Except\+\_\+T Socket\+HTTPClient\+\_\+\+DNSFailed\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



DNS resolution failure. 

Category\+: NETWORK Retryable\+: YES -\/ DNS servers may recover, cache may refresh

Raised when hostname cannot be resolved. May be transient (DNS server overloaded) or permanent (invalid hostname). \Hypertarget{group__http_ga5dc1b9ac7f30436bc422f312cd6db709}\label{group__http_ga5dc1b9ac7f30436bc422f312cd6db709}
